import Alert from "@/components/alert";
import Stat from "@/components/stat";
import BoxPlot, { ComputedBoxPlot } from "@/components/chart/box-plot";
import { formatNumber } from "@/utils/format";

<Alert type="info">The original MANTRA dataset includes both 2-manifolds and 3-manifolds. AHORN lists them as two separate datasets, with this page focusing on the 2-manifolds. You can find the 3-manifolds dataset [here](/dataset/MANTRA-3-manifolds).</Alert>

The MANTRA collection provides simplicial complexes built from triangulations of closed 2- and 3-manifolds.
Each manifold is represented by its vertex set and list of simplices (triangles or tetrahedra), enabling topological and combinatorial experiments across two dimensions.

This dataset is derived from version 0.0.16 of [MANTRA](https://aidos.group/mantra/).

## Dataset Statistics

<dl className="not-prose grid gap-5 sm:grid-cols-2">
  <Stat
    title="Manifolds"
    value={formatNumber(frontmatter["statistics"]["num-manifolds"])}
  />
  <Stat
    title="Simplices (all)"
    value={formatNumber(frontmatter["statistics"]["num-simplices"])}
  />
</dl>

## Size Distribution

<div className="not-prose space-y-4">
  <BoxPlot
    title="Vertices per manifold"
    stats={frontmatter["statistics"]["nodes-boxplot"]}
  />
  <BoxPlot
    title="Simplices per manifold"
    stats={frontmatter["statistics"]["simplices-boxplot"]}
  />
</div>
